Auto-silenced in production. window.__APP_DEBUG__ = false; // Set true for verbose dev logs window.bgLog = function(...args){ if(window.__APP_DEBUG__){ console.log('[BlinkGo]', ...args); } }; window.bgWarn = function(...args){ console.warn('[BlinkGo]', ...args); }; window.bgError = function(...args){ console.error('[BlinkGo]', ...args); }; // === GLOBAL ERROR HANDLERS (prevent app crash) === window.addEventListener('error', (e) => { try { console.error('[BlinkGo Global Error]', e.message, e.filename, e.lineno, e.error); // Show user-friendly toast for uncaught errors (not in production) if(window.__APP_DEBUG__ && typeof showToast === 'function'){ showToast('⚠️ ' + (e.message || 'Unexpected error'), 'error'); } } catch(_) { /* swallow */ } }); window.addEventListener('unhandledrejection', (e) => { try { console.error('[BlinkGo Unhandled Promise]', e.reason); // Don't crash the app on unhandled promise rejections e.preventDefault(); } catch(_) { /* swallow */ } }); // === END GLOBAL ERROR HANDLERS === let state = window.state = { user:null, cart:[], favorites:new Set(), orders:[], // local user orders (customer) notifications:[], currentCat:'all', selectedPay:null, selectedTip:null, trackingOrderId:null, driverOnline:false, driverActiveOrder:null, page:'home', adminTab:'orders', searchQuery:'', simulation:null, // { role:'customer'|'driver', originalUser: {...} } when admin simulates coupons:[], appliedCoupon:null, chatMessages:{}, // { threadKey: [{from:'me'|'them', text, time}] } driverLocations:{}, // { driverId: {x:0..100, y:0..100} } in % of map area reviews:[], // { id, orderId, productId, customerName, rating:1..5, comment, createdAt } dailyCheckin:{ lastDate:null, streak:0, history:[], totalEarned:0 }, wallet:{ balance:0, tx:[] }, // tx: { id, type:'cashback'|'debit', amount, orderId, time } addresses:[], // { id, label, icon, address, isDefault } selectedAddressId:null, referrals:[], // { code, friends:[{name,status:'pending'|'completed',joinedAt}] } badges:[] // ['first_order', 'streak_7', ...] } function t(key){ const dict = TRANSLATIONS[CURRENT_LANG] || TRANSLATIONS.ar; return dict[key] || TRANSLATIONS.ar[key] || key; } // Defensive DOM helpers function safeText(el, txt){ if(el) el.textContent = txt; } function safeStyle(el, prop, val){ if(el && el.style) el.style[prop] = val; } function safeClass(el, method, cls){ try{ if(el && el.classList) el.classList[method](cls); }catch(_){} } /* ============================================================ SECURITY HELPERS — XSS / Injection / Validation BlinkGo: never trust user-controlled strings in templates. ============================================================ */ function esc(s){ // HTML entity escape — for text content & attributes if(s === null || s === undefined) return ''; return String(s) .replace(/&/g, '&') .replace(//g, '>') .replace(/"/g, '"') .replace(/'/g, ''') .replace(/`/g, '`'); } function escId(s){ // For element IDs / map keys / data attributes — alphanumeric + dash + underscore only if(s === null || s === undefined) return ''; return String(s).replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9_\-]/g, '').substring(0, 64); } function escJs(s){ // Safe string for inline onclick="..." with single-quoted value if(s === null || s === undefined) return ''; return String(s) .replace(/\\/g, '\\\\') .replace(/'/g, "\\'") .replace(/"/g, '\\"') .replace(//g, '') .replace(/\n/g, ' ') .replace(/\r/g, '') .substring(0, 80); } function isValidOrder(o){ // Schema-check an order before merging into state.orders if(!o || typeof o !== 'object') return false; // ID can be string OR number (and we coerce to string later) if(o.id === null || o.id === undefined || (typeof o.id !== 'string' && typeof o.id !== 'number')) return false; const idStr = String(o.id); if(idStr.length === 0 || idStr.length > 128) return false; // customerId can be string, number, or null if(o.customerId !== null && o.customerId !== undefined && typeof o.customerId !== 'string' && typeof o.customerId !== 'number') return false; // status must be a valid string if(typeof o.status !== 'string' || !['pending','preparing','delivering','delivered','cancelled','new','accepted','picked_up','arrived'].includes(o.status)) { // Be lenient: accept unknown statuses, just require it to be a string if(typeof o.status !== 'string') return false; } // total: must be a non-negative finite number (optional for pending orders) if(o.total !== undefined && (typeof o.total !== 'number' || !isFinite(o.total) || o.total < 0)) { return false; } // items: must be array if present if(o.items !== undefined && o.items !== null && !Array.isArray(o.items)) { return false; } // No function values for(const k of Object.keys(o)){ const v = o[k]; if(typeof v === 'function') return false; } return true; } function sanitizeOrder(o){ // Strip unknown fields and return a clean copy const clean = {}; // Photo fields need MORE space than text fields (base64 = ~1.4x raw size) const PHOTO_FIELDS = new Set(['deliveryPhoto']); const PHOTO_MAX = 3 * 1024 * 1024; // 3MB per photo (covers ~2MB raw) const TEXT_MAX = 5000; const safeKeys = ['id','customerId','customerName','customerPhone','driverId','driverName','status','items','total','subtotal','deliveryFee','tip','coupon','couponDiscount','address','addressLat','addressLng','driverLat','driverLng','driverBearing','driverUpdatedAt','notes','deliveryPrefs','scheduledFor','refunded','refundedAt','refundReason','createdAt','acceptedAt','pickupAt','arrivedAt','deliveredAt','deliveryPhoto','deliveryPhotoAt','payment','rating','ratingText','emoji','subStatus','updatedAt','pay','merchant']; // Always coerce id to string if(o.id !== undefined) clean.id = String(o.id); for(const k of safeKeys){ if(o[k] !== undefined){ const v = o[k]; if(typeof v === 'string'){ // Photos: allow 3MB; text: 5000 chars const cap = PHOTO_FIELDS.has(k) ? PHOTO_MAX : TEXT_MAX; clean[k] = v.substring(0, cap); } else if(typeof v === 'number') clean[k] = isFinite(v) ? v : null; else if(typeof v === 'boolean') clean[k] = v; else if(typeof v === 'object' && v !== null && !Array.isArray(v) && !(v instanceof Date)) { // Nested object — preserve structure const sub = {}; for(const sk of Object.keys(v).slice(0, 20)){ const sv = v[sk]; if(typeof sv === 'string') sub[sk] = sv.substring(0, 500); else if(typeof sv === 'number') sub[sk] = isFinite(sv) ? sv : null; else sub[sk] = sv; } clean[k] = sub; } else if(Array.isArray(v)) { clean[k] = v.slice(0, 100).map(x => { if(typeof x === 'string') return x.substring(0, 200); if(typeof x === 'number') return isFinite(x) ? x : null; if(x && typeof x === 'object') { // Preserve simple object items (like {id, qty, price, name}) const io = {}; for(const ik of Object.keys(x).slice(0, 10)){ const iv = x[ik]; if(typeof iv === 'string') io[ik] = iv.substring(0, 200); else if(typeof iv === 'number') io[ik] = isFinite(iv) ? iv : null; else io[ik] = iv; } return io; } return null; }).filter(x => x !== null); } } } return clean; } function isSafeKey(k){ // localStorage / Firestore field name validator return typeof k === 'string' && /^[a-zA-Z0-9_\-]{1,64}$/.test(k); } function safeLocalStorageGet(key){ if(!isSafeKey(key)) return null; try{ const raw = localStorage.getItem(key); if(raw === null) return null; // Cap size — reject anything > 6MB to prevent DoS (allows up to 1-2 photos in shared orders) if(raw.length > 6 * 1024 * 1024) return null; return raw; }catch(e){ return null; } } function safeLocalStorageSet(key, value){ if(!isSafeKey(key)) return false; if(typeof value !== 'string') value = String(value); try{ if(value.length > 6 * 1024 * 1024) return false; localStorage.setItem(key, value); return true; }catch(e){ return false; } } function getValidOrders(orders){ // Filter out malformed/oversized order objects before merging if(!Array.isArray(orders)) return []; return orders.filter(isValidOrder).map(sanitizeOrder).filter(Boolean); } // Session security: track idle time & auto-logout let __lastActivityTs = Date.now(); let __sessionWarned = false; ['click','touchstart','keydown','mousemove'].forEach(evt => { document.addEventListener(evt, () => { __lastActivityTs = Date.now(); __sessionWarned = false; }, { passive: true }); }); function __checkSessionIdle(){ const idle = Date.now() - __lastActivityTs; if(state.user && !state.user.offline && idle > 30 * 60 * 1000){ // 30 min idle — log out console.warn('[BlinkGo] Auto-logout: idle 30min'); if(typeof window.doLogout === 'function') window.doLogout(); showToast(CURRENT_LANG==='ar'?'⏱️ تم تسجيل الخروج (نشاط خامل)':'⏱️ Auto-Abmeldung (Inaktivität)'); } else if(state.user && idle > 25 * 60 * 1000 && !__sessionWarned){ __sessionWarned = true; showToast(CURRENT_LANG==='ar'?'⏱️ سيتم تسجيل الخروج خلال 5 دقائق (خامل)':'⏱️ Auto-Abmeldung in 5 Min (Inaktivität)'); } } setInterval(__checkSessionIdle, 60 * 1000); function setLanguage(lang){ try{ if(!TRANSLATIONS[lang]) return; // Update all elements with data-i18n document.querySelectorAll('[data-i18n]').forEach(el => { const key = el.getAttribute('data-i18n'); const v = t(key); if(v && v !== key) el.textContent = v; }); // Update all placeholders with data-i18n-placeholder document.querySelectorAll('[data-i18n-placeholder]').forEach(el => { const key = el.getAttribute('data-i18n-placeholder'); const v = t(key); if(v && v !== key) el.setAttribute('placeholder', v); }); // Update all title attributes with data-i18n-title document.querySelectorAll('[data-i18n-title]').forEach(el => { const key = el.getAttribute('data-i18n-title'); const v = t(key); if(v && v !== key) el.setAttribute('title', v); }); CURRENT_LANG = lang; localStorage.setItem('bg_lang', lang); document.documentElement.setAttribute('lang', lang); document.documentElement.setAttribute('dir', lang === 'ar' ? 'rtl' : 'ltr'); document.body.style.fontFamily = lang === 'ar' ? '"Cairo","Segoe UI",Tahoma,Arial,sans-serif' : '"Inter","Segoe UI","Helvetica Neue",Arial,sans-serif'; // Highlight active lang button try{ const de = document.getElementById('langDeBtn'); const ar = document.getElementById('langArBtn'); if(de && ar){ de.style.background = (lang==='de') ? 'var(--speed-gradient)' : 'transparent'; de.style.color = (lang==='de') ? '#fff' : 'var(--text-muted)'; ar.style.background = (lang==='ar') ? localStorage.setItem('bg_fav', JSON.stringify([...state.favorites])); } function saveSharedOrders(){ try { localStorage.setItem('bg_shared_orders', JSON.stringify(state.orders)); // Last-write timestamp so polling drivers can detect fresh updates localStorage.setItem('bg_shared_orders_ts', String(Date.now())); // Broadcast to other tabs (same browser, works even without Firebase) broadcastOrders(state.orders); } catch(e){ console.warn('[BlinkGo] saveSharedOrders failed:', e); } } function loadSharedOrders(){ try{ return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('bg_shared_orders') || '[]'); }catch(e){ return []; } } // === DEDUPE EXISTING ORDERS === // Removes duplicate orders that may have been created by double-tap // Two orders are considered duplicates if they have: // - Same customerId // - Same items (by id+qty) // - Created within 30 seconds of each other // Keeps the OLDER one (the first that was placed) function dedupeSharedOrders(){ try{ const all = loadSharedOrders(); if(!Array.isArray(all) || all.length < 2) return false; const seen = new Set(); const keep = []; // Sort by createdAt ASC so older comes first const sorted = all.slice().sort((a,b) => (a.createdAt||0) - (b.createdAt||0)); let removed = 0; for(const o of sorted){ if(!o || !o.id){ continue; } // Stronger fingerprint: items + total + customer const itemsFp = (o.items||[]).map(i => `${i.id}x${i.qty||1}`).sort().join('|'); const fingerprint = `${o.customerId}::${o.total}::${itemsFp}`; if(seen.has(fingerprint)){ removed++; console.log('[BlinkGo] Dedup removed duplicate order:', o.id, 'fingerprint:', fingerprint); continue; // skip duplicate } seen.add(fingerprint); keep.push(o); } if(removed > 0){ console.log('[BlinkGo] Dedup removed', removed, 'duplicate orders'); state.orders = keep; saveSharedOrders(); return true; } return false; }catch(e){ console.warn('dedupeSharedOrders failed:', e); return false; } } /* ============================================================ CROSS-TAB / CROSS-DEVICE ORDER BROADCAST - BroadcastChannel API: instant within same browser - storage event: same-browser fallback - Polling: catches Firebase-driven remote updates This means: when customer places an order it reaches the driver on another device through Firebase, OR on the same device instantly. ============================================================ */ window.BG_BROADCAST_CHANNEL = 'blinkgo-orders-v1'; let __bgBroadcastChannel = null; try { if(typeof BroadcastChannel !== 'undefined'){ __bgBroadcastChannel = new BroadcastChannel(window.BG_BROADCAST_CHANNEL); __bgBroadcastChannel.addEventListener('message', (e) => handleBroadcastMessage(e.data)); } } catch(_){} function broadcastOrders(orders, source){ try { if(__bgBroadcastChannel){ __bgBroadcastChannel.postMessage({ type: 'orders:update', orders, source: source||'local', ts: Date.now() }); } // Same-tab fallback via storage event simulation try { // We write the same key — other tabs get `storage` event automatically localStorage.setItem('bg_shared_orders', JSON.stringify(orders)); localStorage.setItem('bg_shared_orders_ts', String(Date.now())); } catch(_){} } catch(e){} } window.__bgBroadcastSeenIds = new Set(); function handleBroadcastMessage(data){ if(!data || !data.type) return; if(data.type === 'orders:update' && Array.isArray(data.orders)){ // Check for new orders that didn't exist in current state const existing = new Set(state.orders.map(o=>o.id)); const trulyNew = data.orders.filter(o => !existing.has(o.id) && !window.__bgBroadcastSeenIds.has(o.id)); trulyNew.forEach(o => window.__bgBroadcastSeenIds.add(o.id)); // Always merge (incoming wins, but keep existing) const merged = mergeOrders(state.orders, data.orders); const myId = state.user?.uid || state.user?.phone; if(state.user?.role === 'driver'){ const before = state.orders.length; state.orders = merged; saveSharedOrders(); if(trulyNew.length > 0){ trulyNew.forEach(o => { if(o.status === 'pending' && !o.driverId){ showIncomingCall(o); } }); renderPageContent(); window.BLINKGO_AUDIO?.chime?.(); } else if(state.orders.length !== before){ renderPageContent(); } } else if(myId){ state.orders = merged.filter(o => (o.customerId === myId) || (o.customerPhone === state.user?.phone)); saveSharedOrders(); renderPageContent(); } } } function mergeOrders(existing, incoming){ // SECURITY: Filter and sanitize incoming orders to prevent malformed data injection const safeIncoming = getValidOrders(incoming); const safeExisting = Array.isArray(existing) ? existing.filter(isValidOrder) : []; const map = new Map(safeExisting.map(o => [String(o.id), o])); // === STATUS PROGRESSION (Wolt pattern) === // Don't let an OLDER status overwrite a NEWER one. // pending < accepted < preparing < delivering < delivered < cancelled const STATUS_RANK = { pending: 0, accepted: 1, preparing: 2, delivering: 3, delivered: 4, cancelled: 5 }; safeIncoming.forEach(o => { const cleaned = sanitizeOrder(o); const id = String(cleaned.id); const existingOrder = map.get(id); if(!existingOrder){ map.set(id, cleaned); return; } // Compare statuses — only overwrite if incoming is >= existing or existing has no driver accepted it const incomingRank = STATUS_RANK[cleaned.status] ?? -1; const existingRank = STATUS_RANK[existingOrder.status] ?? -1; // If existing was accepted/preparing/delivering by THIS driver, don't downgrade if(existingOrder.driverId && existingOrder.driverId === cleaned.driverId && existingRank > incomingRank){ // Keep existing status but update fields like notes/photos map.set(id, { ...cleaned, status: existingOrder.status, subStatus: existingOrder.subStatus, driverId: existingOrder.driverId, driverName: existingOrder.driverName, acceptedAt: existingOrder.acceptedAt, pickedUpAt: existingOrder.pickedUpAt, deliveredAt: existingOrder.deliveredAt }); return; } // Default: merge, incoming wins map.set(id, { ...existingOrder, ...cleaned }); }); return [...map.values()].sort((a,b)=>(b.createdAt||0)-(a.createdAt||0)); } // Cross-tab storage listener window.addEventListener('storage', (e) => { if(e.key === 'bg_shared_orders' && e.newValue){ try { const orders = JSON.parse(e.newValue); handleBroadcastMessage({ type: 'orders:update', orders, source: 'storage-event', ts: Date.now() }); } catch(_){} } }); // === BLINKGO SYNC QUEUE (v4.98) === // Local-first with reliable background sync. Inspired by Wolt/DoorDash patterns. // Pattern: save to localStorage immediately, push to cloud in background, retry on failure. let __bgSyncQueue = []; // [{order, attempts, lastTry}] const __BG_SYNC_MAX_ATTEMPTS = 5; async function bgProcessSyncQueue(){ if(__bgSyncQueue.length === 0) return; const item = __bgSyncQueue[0]; if(Date.now() - item.lastTry < 2000) return; // throttle item.attempts = (item.attempts||0) + 1; item.lastTry = Date.now(); try{ const r = await bgOrderAPI.createOrder(item.order); if(r && r.ok){ console.log('[BlinkGo] ✅ Queue push succeeded for', item.order.id); __bgSyncQueue.shift(); // remove from queue // Update visual indicator const indicator = document.getElementById('bgSyncIndicator'); if(indicator){ indicator.parentElement.classList.remove('bgSyncSyncing'); indicator.parentElement.classList.remove('bgSyncError'); } } else { item.lastTry = Date.now(); if(item.attempts >= __BG_SYNC_MAX_ATTEMPTS){ console.error('[BlinkGo] ❌ Queue push FAILED permanently for', item.order.id); __bgSyncQueue.shift(); const indicator = document.getElementById('bgSyncIndicator'); if(indicator) indicator.parentElement.classList.add('bgSyncError'); } else { console.warn('[BlinkGo] ⚠️ Queue push retry ' + item.attempts + '/' + __BG_SYNC_MAX_ATTEMPTS); } } } catch(e){ item.lastTry = Date.now(); if(item.attempts >= __BG_SYNC_MAX_ATTEMPTS){ console.error('[BlinkGo] ❌ Queue push error permanently:', e?.message); __bgSyncQueue.shift(); } } } function bgEnqueueSync(order){ // Save to localStorage immediately (offline-first) try{ const all = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('bg_pending_sync')||'[]'); all.push(order); localStorage.setItem('bg_pending_sync', JSON.stringify(all)); }catch(_){} __bgSyncQueue.push({ order, attempts: 0, lastTry: 0 }); // Visual: show syncing const indicator = document.getElementById('bgSyncIndicator'); if(indicator) indicator.parentElement.classList.add('bgSyncSyncing'); bgProcessSyncQueue(); // Process queue periodically if(!window.__bgSyncQueueInterval){ window.__bgSyncQueueInterval = setInterval(bgProcessSyncQueue, 3000); } } // On boot, restore pending syncs from localStorage and resume function bgResumePendingSyncs(){ try{ const pending = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('bg_pending_sync')||'[]'); if(pending.length > 0){ console.log('[BlinkGo] Resuming ' + pending.length + ' pending syncs from previous session'); } else { document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => setTimeout(bgResumePendingSyncs, 100)); } // === CUSTOMER POOL POLLING (Wolt pattern) — fallback when Firebase is unavailable === let __bgCustomerPollTimer = null; function startCustomerPoolPolling(){ stopCustomerPoolPolling(); let delay = 4000; const tick = async () => { if(!state.user || state.user.role !== 'customer') return; try { // Pull from Worker pool — only orders for THIS customer const allPool = await bgOrderAPI.getOrders({ status: '' }); if(!Array.isArray(allPool)) return; const myOrders = allPool.filter(o => o.customerId === state.user.uid || o.customerId === state.user.id || o.customerPhone === state.user.phone || (state.user.email && o.customerId === state.user.email) ); if(myOrders.length === 0) return; const before = state.orders.length; const beforeIds = new Set(state.orders.map(o => String(o.id))); state.orders = mergeOrders(state.orders, myOrders); if(state.orders.length !== before){ saveSharedOrders(); // Notify on new orders or status changes myOrders.forEach(o => { const id = String(o.id); if(!beforeIds.has(id)){ bgShowNotification( CURRENT_LANG==='ar' ? '✅ تم استلام طلبك' : '✅ Bestellung empfangen', CURRENT_LANG==='ar' ? `طلب #${id.slice(-6)} في الطريق إلى السائق` : `Bestellung #${id.slice(-6)} geht an Fahrer`, { tag: 'order-upd-'+id, url:'/?track='+id } ); } }); // Re-render if on track page if(state.page === 'track' || state.page === 'orders'){ renderPageContent(); } } delay = 4000; // reset on success } catch(e){ delay = Math.min(delay * 1.5, 15000); // exp backoff on error } finally { __bgCustomerPollTimer = setTimeout(tick, delay); } }; __bgCustomerPollTimer = setTimeout(tick, 1000); // start after 1s } function stopCustomerPoolPolling(){ if(__bgCustomerPollTimer){ clearTimeout(__bgCustomerPollTimer); __bgCustomerPollTimer = null; } } window.startCustomerPoolPolling = startCustomerPoolPolling; window.stopCustomerPoolPolling = stopCustomerPoolPolling; // === PHASE 1 FIX: Global polling manager — kills ALL timers === function bgStopAllPolling(){ try { stopDriverOrderPolling && stopDriverOrderPolling(); } catch(_){} try { stopCustomerPoolPolling && stopCustomerPoolPolling(); } catch(_){} if(window.__bgSyncQueueInterval){ clearInterval(window.__bgSyncQueueInterval); window.__bgSyncQueueInterval = null; } if(window.__bgDriverLocationPolling){ clearInterval(window.__bgDriverLocationPolling); window.__bgDriverLocationPolling = null; } } window.bgStopAllPolling = bgStopAllPolling; // Driver-side polling — Wolt-style SMART polling with exponential backoff. // Pattern: start fast (3s) on initial pickup, then back off (up to 15s) when idle. let __bgDriverPollTimer = null; let __bgDriverFirstPollDone = false; let __bgDriverPollDelay = 3000; // start at 3s const __BG_DRIVER_POLL_MIN = 3000; const __BG_DRIVER_POLL_MAX = 15000; function startDriverOrderPolling(){ stopDriverOrderPolling(); __bgDriverFirstPollDone = false; __bgDriverPollDelay = __BG_DRIVER_POLL_MIN; const tick = async () => { if(!state.user || state.user.role !== 'driver') return; try { const local = loadSharedOrders(); // 1. Always merge local const merged = mergeOrders(state.orders, local); if(JSON.stringify(merged) !== JSON.stringify(state.orders)){ const existingIds = new Set(state.orders.map(o=>o.id)); state.orders = merged; saveSharedOrders(); const fresh = state.orders.filter(o => !existingIds.has(o.id)); if(fresh.length && state.driverOnline){ fresh.forEach(o => { if(o.status === 'pending' && !o.driverId) showIncomingCall(o); }); window.BLINKGO_AUDIO?.chime?.(); } // Only re-render if we're NOT on a stable page (track) // Otherwise the map/list flickers every 2s if(state.page !== 'track' && state.page !== 'home'){ renderPageContent(); } } // 2. Optionally pull from Firebase if available if(typeof firebaseDB !== 'undefined' && firebaseDB){ try { const snap = await firebaseDB.collection('orders') .where('status','in',['pending','preparing','delivering','delivered']) .orderBy('createdAt','desc') .limit(50) .get(); const remote = snap.docs.map(d=>({id:d.id, ...d.data(), createdAt: d.data().createdAt?.toMillis?.() || Date.now()})); const before = state.orders.length; state.orders = mergeOrders(state.orders, remote); if(state.orders.length !== before){ saveSharedOrders(); renderPageContent(); } } catch(e){ /* Firestore may need auth — silently skip */ } } // 3. ALSO pull from Worker order pool (real cross-device sync) — Wolt/Uber Eats pattern try { // First poll: fetch ALL pending orders (no since filter). // Subsequent polls: only fetch new ones from last 60s for efficiency. const poolFilter = __bgDriverFirstPollDone ? { status: 'pending', since: Date.now() - 60000 } : { status: 'pending' }; const pool = await bgOrderAPI.getOrders(poolFilter); if(Array.isArray(pool) && pool.length){ const before = state.orders.length; const beforeIds = new Set(state.orders.map(o => String(o.id))); const merged = mergeOrders(state.orders, pool); state.orders = merged; if(state.orders.length !== before){ saveSharedOrders(); console.log('[BlinkGo] 📥 Driver pulled ' + (state.orders.length - before) + ' new orders from pool (total: ' + state.orders.length + ')'); // Notify driver of new pending orders from pool if(state.driverOnline){ pool.filter(o => o.status === 'pending' && !o.driverId && !beforeIds.has(String(o.id))).forEach(o => { showIncomingCall(o); }); } // Re-render the driver feed on any new order (even on track/home if it's the driver feed) renderPageContent(); } } __bgDriverFirstPollDone = true; } catch(e){ /* Worker may be down — silently skip */ } } catch(e){ console.warn('Driver poll err:', e); } }; // Run immediately with smart backoff const tickWithBackoff = async () => { const before = state.orders.length; await tick(); const after = state.orders.length; if(after > before){ // New order found — reset to fast polling __bgDriverPollDelay = __BG_DRIVER_POLL_MIN; } else { // No change — slowly back off __bgDriverPollDelay = Math.min(__bgDriverPollDelay * 1.3, __BG_DRIVER_POLL_MAX); } __bgDriverPollTimer = setTimeout(tickWithBackoff, __bgDriverPollDelay); }; __bgDriverPollTimer = setTimeout(tickWithBackoff, 0); } function stopDriverOrderPolling(){ if(__bgDriverPollTimer){ clearTimeout(__bgDriverPollTimer); clearInterval(__bgDriverPollTimer); __bgDriverPollTimer = null; } // === PHASE 1 FIX: Reset backoff state === __bgDriverFirstPollDone = false; __bgDriverPollDelay = __BG_DRIVER_POLL_MIN; } function saveSharedNotifications(){ localStorage.setItem('bg_shared_notifs', JSON.stringify(state.notifications)); } function loadSharedNotifications(){ try{ return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('bg_shared_notifs') || '[]'); }catch(e){ return []; } } /* ============================================================ HELPERS ============================================================ */ function $(id){ if(typeof id === 'string') id = id.replace(/^#/, ''); } } window.bgStartBrowserLocation = bgStartBrowserLocation; window.bgStopBrowserLocation = bgStopBrowserLocation; // === PHASE 3 FIX: Image compression for delivery photos === async function bgCompressImage(file, maxWidth, quality){ return new Promise((resolve, reject) => { if(!file || !file.type || !file.type.startsWith('image/')){ reject(new Error('Not an image')); } // === ORDER API — Cloudflare Worker backend === // Provides cross-device order sync via the stripe.blinkgo.de Worker // Falls back gracefully to localStorage if Worker unavailable const BG_ORDER_API_URL = 'https://stripe.blinkgo.de'; try { const params = new URLSearchParams(); if(filter?.status) params.set('status', filter.status); if(filter?.customerId) params.set('customerId', filter.customerId); if(filter?.driverId) params.set('driverId', filter.driverId); this._rateLimitedUntil = Date.now() + backoff; console.warn('[BlinkGo] Worker rate-limited, backing off', backoff/1000, 's'); } this.consecutiveErrors++; return []; } const data = await res.json(); this.consecutiveErrors = 0; if(res.ok){ this.consecutiveErrors = 0; this.lastSyncAt = Date.now(); const data = await res.json().catch(()=>({})); return data.order || merged; } } catch(e){ console.warn('[bgOrderAPI] POST fallback failed:', e?.message); } } if(!res || !res.ok) { this.consecutiveErrors++; this.lastErrorAt = Date.now(); return null; } this.consecutiveErrors = 0; this.lastSyncAt = Date.now(); try { const data = await res.json(); return data.order || null; } catch(_){ return { id, ...updates }; } }, // Quick health check async health(){ try { const res = await fetch(BG_ORDER_API_URL + '/health'); if(!res.ok) return null; return await res.json(); } catch(e){ return null; } }, }; window.bgOrderAPI = bgOrderAPI; /* ============================================================ 📦 REPOSITORY PATTERN — Orders Repository (Phase A.2) - Clean abstraction over the Worker pool - Uses Config + Logger + ErrorService for production-grade - Backward compatible: window.bgOrderAPI still works ============================================================ */ /** * @typedef {Object} Order * @property {string} id * @property {string} customerId * @property {string} customerName * @property {string} customerPhone * @property {string} driverId * @property {string} status - pending|preparing|ready|delivering|delivered|cancelled * @property {Array<{id, name, price, qty}>} items * @property {number} total * @property {number} subtotal * @property {number} deliveryFee * @property {string} address * @property {number} createdAt * @property {string} [deliveryPhoto] */ /** * @typedef {Object} OrderFilter * @property {string} [status] * @property {string} [customerId] * @property {string} [driverId] * @property {number} [since] - timestamp in ms */ class OrdersRepository { /** * @param {Object} [deps] - Dependency injection * @param {string} [deps.baseUrl] - API base URL * @param {Object} [deps.logger] - Logger service * @param {Object} [deps.errorService] - ErrorService * @param {number} [deps.timeoutMs] - Request timeout * @param {number} [deps.maxRetries] - Max retries on failure */ constructor(deps = {}) { this.baseUrl = deps.baseUrl || Config.API.BASE_URL; this.logger = deps.logger || Logger; this.errorService = deps.errorService || ErrorService; this.timeoutMs = deps.timeoutMs || Config.API.TIMEOUT_MS; this.maxRetries = deps.maxRetries || Config.API.RETRY_MAX; this.enabled = true; this.lastSyncAt = 0; this.lastErrorAt = 0; this.consecutiveErrors = 0; } /** * Internal fetch with timeout + error handling * @private */ async _fetch(path, options = {}) { const controller = new AbortController(); const timeoutId = setTimeout(() => controller.abort(), this.timeoutMs); try { const res = await fetch(this.baseUrl + path, { ...options, signal: controller.signal, headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', ...(options.headers || {}) }, }); clearTimeout(timeoutId); if (!res.ok) { const errBody = await res.json().catch(() => ({})); throw this.errorService.create( ErrorCodes.UNKNOWN, `HTTP ${res.status}: ${errBody.error || res.statusText}`, { path, status: res.status, body: errBody } ); } return await res.json(); } catch (err) { clearTimeout(timeoutId); if (err.name === 'AbortError') { throw this.errorService.create(ErrorCodes.NETWORK_TIMEOUT, 'Request timeout', { path }); } throw err; } } /** * Create or update an order in the pool * @param {Order} order * @returns {Promise<{ok: boolean, id: string, order: Order}>} */ async create(order) { if (!this.enabled) return null; if (!order || !order.id) { throw this.errorService.create(ErrorCodes.VALIDATION_FAILED, 'Order must have an id', { order }); } try { const data = await this._fetch('/orders', { method: 'POST', body: JSON.stringify(order), }); this.lastSyncAt = Date.now(); this.consecutiveErrors = 0; this.logger.info('OrdersRepository', `Order ${order.id} created/updated`, { id: order.id }); EventBus.emit('order:created', data); return data; } catch (err) { this.consecutiveErrors++; this.lastErrorAt = Date.now(); this.logger.warn('OrdersRepository', `create failed: ${err.message}`, { id: order.id }); throw err; } } /** * Fetch orders with optional filters * @param {OrderFilter} [filter] * @returns {Promise<Order[]>} */ async findAll(filter = {}) { if (!this.enabled) return []; // === PHASE 5: Rate-limit protection — back off if Worker is overloaded === if (this._rateLimitedUntil && Date.now() < this._rateLimitedUntil) { // Skip this request — Worker still rate-limited return []; } try { const params = new URLSearchParams(); if (filter.status) params.set('status', filter.status); if (filter.customerId) params.set('customerId', filter.customerId); if (filter.driverId) params.set('driverId', filter.driverId); if (filter.since) params.set('since', String(filter.since)); const query = params.toString(); const data = await this._fetch('/orders' + (query ? '?' + query : '')); this.lastSyncAt = Date.now(); this.consecutiveErrors = 0; return data.orders || []; } catch (err) { this.consecutiveErrors++; this.lastErrorAt = Date.now(); // Detect Worker rate limit ("Too many subrequests") const isRateLimit = err && err.message && ( err.message.includes('Too many subrequests') || err.message.includes('429') || err.code === 'E012' ); if (isRateLimit) { // Back off exponentially: 30s, 60s, 120s, max 300s const backoff = Math.min(30000 * Math.pow(2, Math.min(this.consecutiveErrors - 1, 4)), 300000); this._rateLimitedUntil = Date.now() + backoff; this.logger && this.logger.warn('OrdersRepository', `Rate-limited, backing off ${backoff/1000}s`); } else { this.logger && this.logger.warn('OrdersRepository', `findAll failed: ${err.message}`); } return []; // graceful degradation } } /** * Find a single order by id * @param {string} id * @returns {Promise<Order|null>} */ async findById(id) { const orders = await this.findAll(); return orders.find(o => String(o.id) === String(id)) || null; } /** * Check health * @returns {Promise<boolean>} */ async isHealthy() { try { const data = await this._fetch('/health'); return data.status === 'ok'; } catch (err) { return false; } } /** * Get repository stats */ getStats() { return { enabled: this.enabled, lastSyncAt: this.lastSyncAt, lastErrorAt: this.lastErrorAt, consecutiveErrors: this.consecutiveErrors, uptime: this.lastSyncAt ? Date.now() - this.lastSyncAt : null, }; } } // Singleton instance with DI const ordersRepository = new OrdersRepository({ baseUrl: Config.API.BASE_URL, logger: Logger, errorService: ErrorService, }); window.OrdersRepository = OrdersRepository; window.ordersRepository = ordersRepository; // === DRIVER PREFS MODULE (inline fallback) === // Loaded as ./js/services/driver-prefs.js; inlined here for robustness // when served from CDN/cache where module path is missing. if (!AC) return () => {}; if (!_ctx) _ctx = new AC(); const ctx = _ctx; if (ctx.state === 'suspended') ctx.resume(); let t = ctx.currentTime; const oscs = []; mode.pattern.forEach((dur) => { const o = ctx.createOscillator(); // === ANALYTICS — Admin dashboard metrics === async function bgGetAnalytics(){ const now = Date.now(); const dayMs = 24 * 3600 * 1000; const weekMs = 7 * dayMs; const monthMs = 30 * dayMs; const orders = state.orders || []; const completed = orders.filter(o => o.status === 'delivered'); const total = orders.length; const completedCount = completed.length; const cancelledCount = orders.filter(o => o.status === 'cancelled').length; const pendingCount = orders.filter(o => ['pending','preparing','pickup_done','delivering','arrived','scheduled'].includes(o.status)).length; const totalRevenue = completed.reduce((s,o) => s + (o.total||0), 0); const todayRevenue = completed.filter(o => (o.deliveredAt||o.createdAt||0) > now - dayMs).reduce((s,o) => s + (o.total||0), 0); const weekRevenue = completed.filter(o => (o.deliveredAt||o.createdAt||0) > now - weekMs).reduce((s,o) => s + (o.total||0), 0); const monthRevenue = completed.filter(o => (o.deliveredAt||o.createdAt||0) > now - monthMs).reduce((s,o) => s + (o.total||0), 0); const totalTips = completed.reduce((s,o) => s + (o.tip||0), 0); const productCounts = {}; for(const o of completed){ for(const item of (o.items||[])){ productCounts[item.id] = (productCounts[item.id]||0) + (item.qty||1); } } const topProducts = Object.entries(productCounts).sort((a,b) => b[1] - a[1]).slice(0, 5).map(([id, count]) => ({ id, count, name: (typeof getProduct === 'function' ? getProduct(id)?.name : id) || id })); const driverCounts = {}; for(const o of completed){ if(o.driverId) driverCounts[o.driverId] = (driverCounts[o.driverId]||0) + 1; } const topDrivers = Object.entries(driverCounts).sort((a,b) => b[1] - a[1]).slice(0, 5).map(([id, count]) => ({ id, count, name: (typeof DRIVERS !== 'undefined' ? DRIVERS.find(d=>d.id===id)?.name : id) || id })); const ratings = completed.filter(o => o.rating).map(o => o.rating); const avgRating = ratings.length ? (ratings.reduce((s,r)=>s+r,0) / ratings.length) : 0; const refundCount = orders.filter(o => o.refunded).length; const refundTotal = orders.filter(o => o.refunded).reduce((s,o) => s + (o.total||0), 0); return { total, completedCount, cancelledCount, pendingCount, totalRevenue, todayRevenue, weekRevenue, monthRevenue, totalTips, topProducts, topDrivers, avgRating, refundCount, refundTotal, completionRate: total ? (completedCount/total*100) : 0, cancelRate: total ? (cancelledCount/total*100) : 0, }; } window.bgGetAnalytics = bgGetAnalytics; // === DRIVER BONUSES === function bgCalculateBonus(driverId){ const driverOrders = state.orders.filter(o => o.driverId === driverId && o.status === 'delivered'); const lastWeek = Date.now() - 7 * 24 * 3600 * 1000; const recent = driverOrders.filter(o => (o.deliveredAt||o.createdAt||0) > lastWeek); const count = recent.length; let bonus = 0; let tier = '—'; if(count >= 50) { bonus = 50; tier = '⭐ Gold'; } else if(count >= 25) { bonus = 25; tier = '🥈 Silber'; } else if(count >= 10) { bonus = 10; tier = '🥉 Bronze'; } else if(count >= 5) { bonus = 3; tier = '🌱 Starter'; } const totalEarnings = driverOrders.reduce((s,o) => s + (o.total||0) * 0.15 + (o.tip||0), 0); const totalTips = driverOrders.reduce((s,o) => s + (o.tip||0), 0); return { count, bonus, tier, totalEarnings, totalTips }; } window.bgCalculateBonus = bgCalculateBonus; // === SMART DRIVER ASSIGNMENT === async function bgFindClosestDriver(lat, lng, excludeIds = []){ if(typeof DRIVERS === 'undefined') return null; let best = null; let bestDist = Infinity; for(const d of DRIVERS){ if(excludeIds.includes(d.id)) continue; const dLat = d.lat || (51.2277 + (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.1); const dLng = d.lng || (6.7735 + (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.2); const R = 6371; const dLatRad = (lat - dLat) * Math.PI / 180; const dLngRad = (lng - dLng) * Math.PI / 180; const a = Math.sin(dLatRad/2) * Math.sin(dLatRad/2) + Math.cos(dLat * Math.PI / 180) * Math.cos(lat * Math.PI / 180) * Math.sin(dLngRad/2) * Math.sin(dLngRad/2); const dist = R * 2 * Math.atan2(Math.sqrt(a), Math.sqrt(1-a)); if(dist < bestDist){ bestDist = dist; best = { ...d, distance: dist }; } } return best; } window.bgFindClosestDriver = bgFindClosestDriver; // === INPUT VALIDATION === function bgValidateInput(value, type, opts){ if(value === null || value === undefined) return false; const v = String(value).trim(); if(!v) return false; switch(type){ case 'email': return /^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/.test(v); === // Centralized earnings logic — used by earnings page + dashboard function bgDriverEarnings(orders){ const L = CURRENT_LANG === 'ar'; const myId = currentDriverId(); const delivered = (orders||state.orders).filter(o => o.driverId===myId && o.status==='delivered'); const COMMISSION = 0.15; // driver gets 15% commission const dayMs = 86400000; const now = Date.now(); const startOfToday = new Date(); startOfToday.setHours(0,0,0,0); const startOfTodayMs = startOfToday.getTime(); const startOfWeekMs = startOfTodayMs - 6*dayMs; // 7 days back const startOfMonthMs = startOfTodayMs - 29*dayMs; // 30 days back function byPay(list){ const card = [], cash = [], wallet = []; for(const o of list){ const p = (o.payment || o.pay || 'cash').toLowerCase(); if(p === 'card' || p === 'stripe') card.push(o); else if(p === 'wallet') wallet.push(o); else cash.push(o); } return {card, cash, wallet}; } function earningsOf(o){ return Math.round((o.total||0) * COMMISSION) + (o.tip||0); } const allDelivered = delivered; const todayDelivered = delivered.filter(o => (o.deliveredAt||o.createdAt||0) >= startOfTodayMs); const weekDelivered = delivered.filter(o => (o.deliveredAt||o.createdAt||0) >= startOfWeekMs); const monthDelivered = delivered.filter(o => (o.deliveredAt||o.createdAt||0) >= startOfMonthMs); function statsFor(list){ const total = list.reduce((s,o)=>s+earningsOf(o),0); const tips = list.reduce((s,o)=>s+(o.tip||0),0); const base = list.reduce((s,o)=>s+Math.round((o.total||0)*COMMISSION),0); const {card, cash, wallet} = byPay(list); const paid = list.filter(o => o.paid === true || o.paymentStatus === 'paid').length; return { total, tips, base, count: list.length, paid, unpaid: list.length - paid, card: {count: card.length, sum: card.reduce((s,o)=>s+earningsOf(o),0)}, cash: {count: cash.length, sum: cash.reduce((s,o)=>s+earningsOf(o),0)}, wallet: {count: wallet.length, sum: wallet.reduce((s,o)=>s+earningsOf(o),0)}, }; } return { all: statsFor(allDelivered), today: statsFor(todayDelivered), week: statsFor(weekDelivered), month: statsFor(monthDelivered), recentOrders: [...allDelivered].sort((a,b) => (b.deliveredAt||b.createdAt||0) - (a.deliveredAt||a.createdAt||0)).slice(0,10), earningsOf, commission: COMMISSION, }; } /* === LEAFLET MAP (Live Tracking) === */ const lng2){ const R = 6371; const dLat = (lat2 - lat1) * Math.PI / 180; const dLng = (lng2 - lng1) * Math.PI / 180; const a = Math.sin(dLat/2) * Math.sin(dLat/2) + Math.cos(lat1 * Math.PI / 180) * Math.cos(lat2 * Math.PI / 180) * Math.sin(dLng/2) * Math.sin(dLng/2); return R * 2 * Math.atan2(Math.sqrt(a), Math.sqrt(1-a)); } // Bearing function bgBearing(lat1, lng1, lat2, lng2){ const y = Math.sin((lng2 - lng1) * Math.PI / 180) * Math.cos(lat2 * Math.PI / 180); const x = Math.cos(lat1 * Math.PI / 180) * Math.sin(lat2 * Math.PI / 180) - Math.sin(lat1 * Math.PI / 180) * Math.cos(lat2 * Math.PI / 180) * Math.cos((lng2 - lng1) * Math.PI / 180); return (Math.atan2(y, x) * 180 / Math.PI + 360) % 360; } // Create SVG marker icon function bgMakeMarkerIcon(type, bearing, label){ if(type const maxLng = Math.max(...allLngs) + padLng; // Linear interpolation to pixel coordinates (0-100% of container) const latToY = (lat) => ((maxLat - lat) / (maxLat - minLat)) * 100; const lngToX = (lng) => ((lng - minLng) / (maxLng - minLng)) * 100; } } /* ============================================================ DATA ACCESS (CROSS-ROLE SHARED) ============================================================ */ function loadCustomerOrders(){ // === START CUSTOMER POOL POLLING (Wolt pattern) — real-time status updates === startCustomerPoolPolling(); } banner.innerHTML = _renderSimBanner(); renderPageContent(); } function setActivePage(page){ try{ // Haptic feedback on navigation if(navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate(5); state.page = page; document.querySelectorAll('.b-nav-item').forEach(b=>{ b.classList.toggle('active', b.dataset.page===page); }catch(e){} }catch(err){ console.error('setActivePage error:', err, 'page:', page); showToast(CURRENT_LANG==='ar'?'❌ خطأ في التنقل':'❌ Navigationsfehler'); // Reset rendering flag _rendering = false; } } function renderPageContent(){ if(_rendering) return; // === DEBOUNCE: Prevent render storms === if(window.__bgRenderTimer){ clearTimeout(window.__bgRenderTimer); } // Use microtask for sub-millisecond deferral return new Promise(resolve => { window.__bgRenderTimer = setTimeout(() => { _doRenderPageContent(); resolve(); }, 16); // ~60fps }); } function _doRenderPageContent(){ if(_rendering) return; _rendering = true; try{ const c = $('content'); if(!c) return; // === GLOBAL DEDUP: Clean state.orders on every render (sledgehammer) === // Removes orders that are duplicates based on customer + items + total within last 5 minutes if(state.orders && state.orders.length > 1){ const seen = new Map(); const deduped = []; // Sort by createdAt DESC (newest first) so we keep the newest duplicate const sorted = state.orders.slice().sort((a,b) => (b.createdAt||0) - (a.createdAt||0)); for(const o of sorted){ if(!o || !o.id) { deduped.push(o); continue; } const itemsFp = (o.items||[]).map(i => `${i.id}x${i.qty||1}`).sort().join('|'); const fp = `${o.customerId||'guest'}::${o.total}::${itemsFp}`; const now = Date.now(); // Only dedupe if within 5 minutes (don't touch old completed orders) if((now - (o.createdAt||0)) < 300000 && seen.has(fp)){ console.log('[BlinkGo] RENDER DEDUP: removing duplicate', o.id); continue; } seen.set(fp, o.id); deduped.push(o); } if(deduped.length !== state.orders.length){ state.orders = deduped; try { saveSharedOrders(); } catch(_){} } } // If no user is logged in, just leave content empty (auth screen shows by default) if(!state.user) return; if(o && o.status === 'delivered'){ setActivePage('orders'); } else { setActivePage('track'); } } window.renderReceipt = renderReceipt; window.bgRenderReceipt = renderReceipt; function bgViewReceipt(orderId){ const o = state.orders.find(x => String(x.id) === String(orderId)); window.printReceipt = printReceipt; window.bgShareReceipt = bgShareReceipt; window.goBackFromReceipt = goBackFromReceipt; // === CUSTOMER MAP: initialize and update with driver location === async function bgInitCustomerMap(orderId){ try { return await _bgInitCustomerMapImpl(orderId); } catch(err) { console.warn('[bgInitCustomerMap] Error:', err.message); // Don't crash - show fallback background const container = document.getElementById('bgCustomerMap'); if(container){ container.innerHTML = '<div style="position:absolute;inset:0;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;background:linear-gradient(135deg,#0a3050,#082540);color:#7fb3d5;font-size:14px;font-weight:600;flex-direction:column;gap:10px;border-radius:20px"><div style="width:36px;height:36px;border:3px solid rgba(0,157,224,.3);border-top-color:#009DE0;border-radius:50%;animation:spin 1s linear infinite"></div>'+(CURRENT_LANG==='ar'?'الخريطة قيد التحميل...':'Karte wird geladen...')+'</div>'; } return false; } } async function _bgInitCustomerMapImpl(orderId){ const container = document.getElementById('bgCustomerMap'); if(!container) return false; const o = (state.orders||[]).find(x => String(x.id) === String(orderId)); if(!o) return false; // Hide loading overlay (static map is now showing) const loadingOverlay = document.getElementById('bgMapLoadingOverlay'); if(loadingOverlay) loadingOverlay.style.display = 'none'; // Update overlay markers with Wolt-style design try { bgUpdateMapOverlay(orderId); } catch(_) {} const osmFrame = document.getElementById('bgCustomerMapOSM'); if(osmFrame) osmFrame.style.display = 'none'; const mapCfg = bgGetMapCenter(); let destLat = mapCfg.lat, destLng = mapCfg.lng; try { const cust = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('bg_user_location') || 'null'); if(cust && typeof cust.lat === 'number' && cust.label && cust.label !== 'default' && cust.label !== 'search'){ destLat = cust.lat; destLng = cust.lng; } else if(o.addressLat && o.addressLng){ destLat = o.addressLat; destLng = o.addressLng; } } catch(_){} let driverLat = null, driverLng = null; if(o.driverLat && o.driverLng){ driverLat = o.driverLat; driverLng = o.driverLng; } const loading = container.querySelector('.bg-map-loading'); if(loading) loading.remove(); // === SAFETY FALLBACK: ensure container is visible === container.style.cssText += 'position:relative;overflow:hidden;background:linear-gradient(135deg,#0a1a2e 0%,#1a2942 50%,#0a0a0f 100%);min-height:340px;'; // === AUTO-FIT: pick zoom that shows both markers with good margin === let currentZoom = (typeof state.bgMapZoom === 'number' && state.bgMapZoomManual) ? state.bgMapZoom : 15; if(driverLat !== null && !state.bgMapZoomManual){ const R = 6371; const dLat = (driverLat - destLat) * Math.PI / 180; const dLng = (driverLng - destLng) * Math.PI / 180; const a = Math.sin(dLat/2) * Math.sin(dLat/2) + Math.cos(destLat * Math.PI / 180) * Math.cos(driverLat * Math.PI / 180) * Math.sin(dLng/2) * Math.sin(dLng/2); const distanceKm = R * 2 * Math.atan2(Math.sqrt(a), Math.sqrt(1-a)); // Pick zoom so both fit in 2x2 grid comfortably if(distanceKm > 10) currentZoom = 11; else if(distanceKm > 5) currentZoom = 12; else if(distanceKm > 2) currentZoom = 13; else if(distanceKm > 1) currentZoom = 14; else if(distanceKm > 0.4) currentZoom = 15; else if(distanceKm > 0.15) currentZoom = 16; else currentZoom = 17; state.bgMapZoom = currentZoom; } else if(!state.bgMapZoomManual){ // No driver - just show customer at z15 currentZoom = 15; state.bgMapZoom = 15; } // === GRID SELECTION: 2x2 if no driver, 3x3 with driver === const hasDriver = (driverLat !== null); const gridSize = hasDriver ? 3 : 2; // 3x3 with driver, 2x2 without const gridOffset = hasDriver ? 1 : 0; const tileSize = 256; const gridPx = gridSize * tileSize; // 768 or 512 // === CENTER: customer at center for no driver, midpoint for driver === const centerLat = hasDriver ? (driverLat + destLat) / 2 : destLat; const centerLng = hasDriver ? (driverLng + destLng) / 2 : destLng; const z = currentZoom; // === TILE COORDS === const tx = Math.floor((centerLng + 180) / 360 * Math.pow(2, z)); const ty = Math.floor((1 - Math.log(Math.tan(centerLat * Math.PI / 180) + 1 / Math.cos(centerLat * Math.PI / 180)) / Math.PI) / 2 * Math.pow(2, z)); // === BUILD TILE HTML (3x3 or 2x2) === let tilesHTML = ''; for(let dy = 0; dy < gridSize; dy++){ for(let dx = 0; dx < gridSize; dx++){ const ttx = tx + dx - gridOffset; const tty = ty + dy - gridOffset; const tsub = ['a','b','c','d'][(ttx + tty) & 3]; const url = `https://cartodb-basemaps-${tsub}.global.ssl.fastly.net/dark_all/${z}/${ttx}/${tty}.png`; const leftPos = (dx - gridOffset) * tileSize; const topPos = (dy - gridOffset) * tileSize; // Validate tile coords const maxTile = Math.pow(2, z); if(ttx < 0 || tty < 0 || ttx >= maxTile || tty >= maxTile){ tilesHTML += `<div style="position:absolute;left:${leftPos}px;top:${topPos}px;width:${tileSize}px;height:${tileSize}px;background:#0a3050;pointer-events:none;z-index:1"></div>`; } else { // Use OSM tiles (more reliable than Carto) const osmUrl = `https://tile.openstreetmap.org/${z}/${ttx}/${tty}.png`; tilesHTML += `<img src="${osmUrl}" data-tile style="position:absolute;left:${leftPos}px;top:${topPos}px;width:${tileSize}px;height:${tileSize}px;pointer-events:none;user-select:none;z-index:1;filter:brightness(.55) contrast(1.15) saturate(.7) hue-rotate(180deg);mix-blend-mode:luminosity" alt="" decoding="async" crossorigin="anonymous" onerror="this.style.display='none'">`; } } } // === POSITION CALCULATIONS === // Fractional position of points within their tile const frac = (lat, lng) => { return { x: ((lng + 180) / 360 * Math.pow(2, z) - Math.floor((lng + 180) / 360 * Math.pow(2, z))) * tileSize, y: ((1 - Math.log(Math.tan(lat * Math.PI / 180) + 1 / Math.cos(lat * Math.PI / 180)) / Math.PI) / 2 * Math.pow(2, z) - Math.floor((1 - Math.log(Math.tan(lat * Math.PI / 180) + 1 / Math.cos(lat * Math.PI / 180)) / Math.PI) / 2 * Math.pow(2, z))) * tileSize }; }; const destF = frac(destLat, destLng); const centerF = frac(centerLat, centerLng); // Customer position relative to grid center const custLeft = destF.x - centerF.x; const custTop = destF.y - centerF.y; // === DISTANCE + BEARING === let distanceBadgeHTML = ''; let routeLineHTML = ''; let driverMarkerHTML = ''; let bearingText = ''; if(hasDriver){ const R = 6371; const dLat = (driverLat - destLat) * Math.PI / 180; const dLng = (driverLng - destLng) * Math.PI / 180; const a = Math.sin(dLat/2) * Math.sin(dLat/2) + Math.cos(destLat * Math.PI / 180) * Math.cos(driverLat * Math.PI / 180) * Math.sin(dLng/2) * Math.sin(dLng/2); const distanceKm = R * 2 * Math.atan2(Math.sqrt(a), Math.sqrt(1-a)); const avgSpeed = 25; const etaMin = Math.max(1, Math.round((distanceKm / avgSpeed) * 60)); // Bearing from driver to customer const y = Math.sin((destLng - driverLng) * Math.PI / 180) * Math.cos(destLat * Math.PI / 180); const x = Math.cos(driverLat * Math.PI / 180) * Math.sin(destLat * Math.PI / 180) - Math.sin(driverLat * Math.PI / 180) * Math.cos(destLat * Math.PI / 180) * Math.cos((destLng - driverLng) * Math.PI / 180); const bearing = (Math.atan2(y, x) * 180 / Math.PI + 360) % 360; bearingText = Math.round(bearing) + '°'; distanceBadgeHTML = `<div style="position:absolute;top:14px;left:50%;transform:translateX(-50%);z-index:1000;background:rgba(10,10,10,.85);color:#fff;padding:8px 16px;border-radius:99px;font-size:12px;font-weight:700;backdrop-filter:blur(12px);border:1px solid rgba(0,157,224,.4);box-shadow:0 6px 20px rgba(0,0,0,.5);display:flex;align-items:center;gap:10px;pointer-events:none"> <i class="fas fa-route" style="color:#009DE0;font-size:13px"></i> <span style="color:#009DE0;font-size:13px;font-weight:900">${distanceKm < 1 ? Math.round(distanceKm*1000) + ' m' : distanceKm.toFixed(distanceKm < 10 ? 2 : 1) + ' km'}</span> <div style="width:1px;height:14px;background:rgba(255,255,255,.2)"></div> <i class="fas fa-clock" style="color:#fff;font-size:11px"></i> <span style="font-weight:800">~${etaMin} min</span> </div>`; // Driver position (clamped to visible area for far distances) const drvF = frac(driverLat, driverLng); let drvLeft = drvF.x - centerF.x; let drvTop = drvF.y - centerF.y; // Clamp to ±140px from center for visibility when distance > 5km if(distanceKm > 5){ const maxOffset = 140; const angle = Math.atan2(drvTop, drvLeft); const dist = Math.sqrt(drvLeft*drvLeft + drvTop*drvTop); if(dist > maxOffset){ drvLeft = Math.cos(angle) * maxOffset; drvTop = Math.sin(angle) * maxOffset; } } let custLeftR = custLeft; custTopR = Math.sin(angle) * maxOffset; } } // WOLT-STYLE Route line (animated dashes, blue) const dx = custLeftR - drvLeft; const dy = custTopR - drvTop; const routeLength = Math.sqrt(dx*dx + dy*dy); const routeAngle = Math.atan2(dy, dx) * 180 / Math.PI; if(routeLength > 4){ routeLineHTML = ` <!-- Wolt-style outer glow --> <div style="position:absolute;left:calc(50% + ${drvLeft}px);top:calc(50% + ${drvTop - 2}px);width:${routeLength}px;height:6px;background:rgba(0,157,224,.18);transform-origin:0 50%;transform:rotate(${routeAngle}deg);z-index:48;border-radius:3px;pointer-events:none"></div> <!-- Animated dashes line --> <div class="wolt-route-line" style="position:absolute;left:calc(50% + ${drvLeft}px);top:calc(50% + ${drvTop}px);width:${routeLength}px;height:3px;background:repeating-linear-gradient(90deg,#009DE0 0px,#009DE0 8px,transparent 8px,transparent 16px);background-size:16px 100%;transform-origin:0 50%;transform:rotate(${routeAngle}deg);z-index:49;border-radius:2px;animation:woltRouteFlow 1s linear infinite;pointer-events:none"></div> <!-- Endpoints --> <div style="position:absolute;left:calc(50% + ${drvLeft - 4}px);top:calc(50% + ${drvTop - 4}px);width:8px;height:8px;background:#009DE0;border-radius:50%;z-index:50;box-shadow:0 0 8px rgba(0,157,224,.6);pointer-events:none"></div> <div style="position:absolute;left:calc(50% + ${custLeftR - 4}px);top:calc(50% + ${custTopR - 4}px);width:8px;height:8px;background:#00C853;border-radius:50%;z-index:50;box-shadow:0 0 8px rgba(0,200,83,.6);pointer-events:none"></div>`; } // WOLT-STYLE Driver marker (blue circle with bearing arrow + pulse) const driverName = (typeof DRIVERS !== 'undefined' ? (DRIVERS.find(d=>d.id===o.driverId)||{}) : ({})) || {}; const drvInitials = (driverName.name||'D').split(' ').map(x=>(x||'')[0]).join('').substring(0,2).toUpperCase(); driverMarkerHTML = ` <div style="position:absolute;left:calc(50% + ${drvLeft}px);top:calc(50% + function bgAnimateDriverMarker(driverEl, fromLat, fromLng, toLat, toLng, fromBearing, toBearing, duration = 4000){ // Cancel any active animation if(window.__bgDriverMarkerAnim){ cancelAnimationFrame(window.__bgDriverMarkerAnim); window.__bgDriverMarkerAnim = null; } const startTime = performance.now(); function step(now){ const elapsed = now - startTime; const t = Math.min(1, elapsed / duration); // Linear interpolation for LatLng const curLat = fromLat + (toLat - fromLat) * t; const curLng = fromLng + (toLng - fromLng) * t; // Bearing interpolation (handle wrap-around) let bDelta = toBearing - fromBearing; if(bDelta > 180) bDelta -= 360; if(bDelta < -180) bDelta += 360; const curBearing = fromBearing + bDelta * t; // Update position via CSS variable (no re-render) driverEl.style.setProperty('--driver-lat', curLat); driverEl.style.setProperty('--driver-lng', curLng); driverEl.style.setProperty('--driver-bearing', curBearing + 'deg'); if(t < 1){ window.__bgDriverMarkerAnim = requestAnimationFrame(step); } else { window.__bgDriverMarkerAnim = null; } } window.__bgDriverMarkerAnim = requestAnimationFrame(step); } // Get interpolated driver position from CSS vars (or fallback) function bgGetInterpolatedDriverPos(){ const lat = parseFloat(document.documentElement.style.getPropertyValue('--driver-lat')); const lng = parseFloat(document.documentElement.style.getPropertyValue('--driver-lng')); return (isNaN(lat) || isNaN(lng)) ? null : {lat, lng}; } // Zoom controls function bgMapZoomIn(){ state.bgMapZoomManual = true; if(typeof state.bgMapZoom === 'number'){ state.bgMapZoom = Math.min(18, state.bgMapZoom + 1); } else { state.bgMapZoom = 16; } if(state.trackingOrderId) bgInitCustomerMap(state.trackingOrderId); } function bgMapZoomOut(){ state.bgMapZoomManual = true; if(typeof state.bgMapZoom === 'number'){ state.bgMapZoom = Math.max(10, state.bgMapZoom - 1); } else { state.bgMapZoom = 14; } if(state.trackingOrderId) bgInitCustomerMap(state.trackingOrderId); } function bgMapRecenter(){ state.bgMapZoomManual = false; state.bgMapZoom = null; // Will be auto-set if(state.trackingOrderId) bgInitCustomerMap(state.trackingOrderId); } window.bgMapZoomIn = bgMapZoomIn; window.bgMapZoomOut = bgMapZoomOut; window.bgMapRecenter = bgMapRecenter; // Zoom controls function bgMapZoomIn(){ if(typeof state.bgMapZoom === 'number'){ state.bgMapZoom = Math.min(18, state.bgMapZoom + 1); } else { state.bgMapZoom = 16; } if(state.trackingOrderId) bgInitCustomerMap(state.trackingOrderId); // bearing window.__bgDriverGPSEnabled = false; var __bgDriverGPSEnabled = false; window.__bgDriverMyLat = __bgDriverMyLat; window.__bgDriverMyLng = __bgDriverMyLng; function bgStartDriverGPS(){ if(!navigator.geolocation){ showToast(CURRENT_LANG==='ar'?'❌ GPS غير مدعوم':'❌ GPS nicht verfügbar'); return false; } if(__bgDriverMyWatchId !== null) return true; // already running __bgDriverMyWatchId = navigator.geolocation.watchPosition( (pos) => { __bgDriverMyLat = pos.coords.latitude; __bgDriverMyLng = pos.coords.longitude; } function bgStopDriverGPS(){ if(__bgDriverMyWatchId !== null){ navigator.geolocation.clearWatch(__bgDriverMyWatchId); __bgDriverMyWatchId = null; } __bgDriverGPSEnabled = false; } // Simulate driver moving toward customer (for testing without real GPS) function bgSimulateDriverMove(targetLat, targetLng, stepKm){ stepKm = stepKm || 0.05; // 50m steps const R = 6371; const dLat = (targetLat - __bgDriverMyLat) * Math.PI / 180; const dLng = (targetLng - __bgDriverMyLng) * Math.PI / 180; const a = Math.sin(dLat/2) * Math.sin(dLat/2) + Math.cos(__bgDriverMyLat * Math.PI / 180) * Math.cos(targetLat * Math.PI / 180) * Math.sin(dLng/2) * Math.sin(dLng/2); const c = 2 * Math.atan2(Math.sqrt(a), Math.sqrt(1-a)); const totalKm = R * c; if(totalKm < stepKm){ __bgDriverMyLat = targetLat; __bgDriverMyLng = targetLng; } else { const ratio = stepKm / totalKm; __bgDriverMyLat = __bgDriverMyLat + (targetLat - __bgDriverMyLat) * ratio; __bgDriverMyLng = __bgDriverMyLng + (targetLng - __bgDriverMyLng) * ratio; } window.__bgDriverMyLat = __bgDriverMyLat; window.__bgDriverMyLng = __bgDriverMyLng; // Push to Worker so customer sees live update if(window.__bgDriverActiveOrderId && typeof bgOrderAPI !== 'undefined' && bgOrderAPI.enabled){ bgOrderAPI.updateOrder(window.__bgDriverActiveOrderId, { driverLat: __bgDriverMyLat, driverLng: __bgDriverMyLng, driverUpdatedAt: Date.now() }).catch(()=>{}); } } // Initialize driver navigation map function bgInitDriverMap(orderId){ const container = document.getElementById('bgDriverMap'); if(!container) return; const o = state.orders.find(x => String(x.id) === String(orderId)); custLng = o.addressLng; custLabel = o.address || ''; } else { try { const cust = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('bg_user_location') || 'null'); if(cust && cust.lat && cust.lng){ custLat = cust.lat; custLng = cust.lng; custLabel = cust.label || ''; } else { const mapCfg = bgGetMapCenter(); custLat = mapCfg.lat; custLng = mapCfg.lng; custLabel = mapCfg.label || ''; } } catch(_){ const mapCfg = bgGetMapCenter(); custLat = mapCfg.lat; custLng = mapCfg.lng; custLabel = mapCfg.label || ''; } } // Center between driver and customer const centerLat = (__bgDriverMyLat + custLat) / 2; const centerLng = (__bgDriverMyLng + custLng) / 2; // Choose zoom to fit both markers const R = 6371; const dLat = (custLat - __bgDriverMyLat) * Math.PI / 180; const dLng = (custLng - __bgDriverMyLng) * Math.PI / 180; const a = Math.sin(dLat/2) * Math.sin(dLat/2) + Math.cos(__bgDriverMyLat * Math.PI / 180) * Math.cos(custLat * Math.PI / 180) * Math.sin(dLng/2) * Math.sin(dLng/2); const distanceKm = R * 2 * Math.atan2(Math.sqrt(a), Math.sqrt(1-a)); // Auto-zoom based on distance let z = 15; if(distanceKm > 500) z = 6; // Cross-country else if(distanceKm > 100) z = 8; // State-level else if(distanceKm > 30) z = 10; else if(distanceKm > 10) z = 11; else if(distanceKm > 5) z = 12; else if(distanceKm > 2) z = 13; else if(distanceKm > 1) z = 14; else if(distanceKm > 0.5) z = 15; else if(distanceKm > 0.2) z = 16; else z = 17; if(typeof state.bgDriverMapZoom === 'number') z = state.bgDriverMapZoom; container.style.height = '320px'; container.style.width = '100%'; container.style.position = 'relative'; container.style.borderRadius = '14px'; container.style.overflow = 'hidden'; container.style.background = '#1a1a1a'; // Build 3x3 tile grid (768x768) to cover wider area const tx = Math.floor((centerLng + 180) / 360 * Math.pow(2, z)); const ty = Math.floor((1 - Math.log(Math.tan(centerLat * Math.PI / 180) + 1 / Math.cos(centerLat * Math.PI / 180)) / Math.PI) / 2 * Math.pow(2, z)); let tilesHTML = ''; for(let dy = -1; dy <= 1; dy++){ for(let dx = -1; dx <= 1; dx++){ const ttx = tx + dx; const tty = ty + dy; const tsub = ['a','b','c','d'][(ttx + tty) & 3]; const url = `https://cartodb-basemaps-${tsub}.global.ssl.fastly.net/dark_all/${z}/${ttx}/${tty}.png`; const leftPos = (dx + 1) * 256; const topPos = (dy + 1) * 256; tilesHTML += `<img src="${url}" style="position:absolute;left:${leftPos}px;top:${topPos}px;width:256px;height:256px;pointer-events:none;user-select:none;z-index:1" alt="" loading="lazy" onerror="this.style.background='rgba(255,107,0,0.3)';this.style.opacity='0.5'">`; } } // Calculate pixel positions const centerFracX = ((centerLng + 180) / 360 * Math.pow(2, z)) - tx; const centerFracY = ((1 - Math.log(Math.tan(centerLat * Math.PI / 180) + 1 / Math.cos(centerLat * Math.PI / 180)) / Math.PI) / 2 * Math.pow(2, z)) - ty; const centerXInGrid = centerFracX * 256; const centerYInGrid = centerFracY * 256; const gridStyle = `position:absolute;left:calc(50% - ${centerXInGrid}px);top:calc(50% - ${centerYInGrid}px);width:768px;height:768px;z-index:1;pointer-events:none`; // Driver position const dFracX = ((__bgDriverMyLng + 180) / 360 * Math.pow(2, z)) - tx; const dFracY = ((1 - Math.log(Math.tan(__bgDriverMyLat * Math.PI / 180) + 1 / Math.cos(__bgDriverMyLat * Math.PI / 180)) / Math.PI) / 2 * Math.pow(2, z)) - ty; const driverLeft = (dFracX - centerFracX) * 256; const driverTop = (dFracY - centerFracY) * 256; // Customer position const cFracX = ((custLng + 180) / 360 * Math.pow(2, z)) - tx; const cFracY = ((1 - Math.log(Math.tan(custLat * Math.PI / 180) + 1 / Math.cos(custLat * Math.PI / 180)) / Math.PI) / 2 * Math.pow(2, z)) - ty; const custLeft = (cFracX - centerFracX) * 256; const custTop = (cFracY - centerFracY) * 256; // Distance + ETA const avgSpeed = 25; const etaMin = Math.max(1, Math.round((distanceKm / avgSpeed) * 60)); // Bearing from driver to customer const y = Math.sin((custLng - __bgDriverMyLng) * Math.PI / 180) * Math.cos(custLat * Math.PI / 180); const x = Math.cos(__bgDriverMyLat * Math.PI / 180) * Math.sin(custLat * Math.PI / 180) - Math.sin(__bgDriverMyLat * Math.PI / 180) * Math.cos(custLat * Math.PI / 180) * Math.cos((custLng - __bgDriverMyLng) * Math.PI / 180); const bearing = (Math.atan2(y, x) * 180 / Math.PI + 360) % 360; // Route line from driver to customer const dx = custLeft - driverLeft; const dy = custTop - driverTop; const routeLength = Math.sqrt(dx*dx + dy*dy); const routeAngle = Math.atan2(dy, dx) * 180 / Math.PI; // Calculate route polyline dots (dashes along the line) let routeDotsHTML = ''; if(routeLength > 30){ const numDots = Math.floor(routeLength / 20); for(let i = 1; i < numDots; i++){ const ratio = i / numDots; const dotX = driverLeft + dx * ratio; const dotY = driverTop + dy * ratio; routeDotsHTML += `<div style="position:absolute;left:calc(50% + ${dotX}px);top:calc(50% + ${dotY}px);width:4px;height:4px;background:rgba(255,107,0,.5);border-radius:50%;transform:translate(-50%,-50%);z-index:48"></div>`; } } let routeLineHTML = ''; if(routeLength > 8){ routeLineHTML = `<div style="position:absolute;left:calc(50% + ${driverLeft}px);top:calc(50% + ${driverTop}px);width:${routeLength}px;height:4px;background:linear-gradient(90deg,rgba(255,107,0,.8) 0%,rgba(255,107,0,.8) 100%);transform-origin:0 50%;transform:rotate(${routeAngle}deg);z-index:48;border-radius:2px"></div> ${routeDotsHTML}`; } // Driver marker (motorcycle) with bearing const driverHTML = `<div id="bgDriverMapMarker" style="position:absolute;left:calc(50% + ${driverLeft}px - 22px);top:calc(50% + ${driverTop}px - 44px);z-index:200;transition:left 1.2s ease,top 1.2s ease;filter:drop-shadow(0 4px 8px rgba(0,0,0,.5))"> <div style="position:relative;width:44px;height:44px"> <div style="position:absolute;inset:0;background:linear-gradient(135deg,#FF6B00,#FF1744);width:44px;height:44px;border-radius:50%;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;color:#fff;font-size:20px;border:3px solid #fff;box-shadow:0 4px 12px rgba(0,0,0,.5);animation:bgDriverPulse 1.5s ease-in-out infinite"> <i class="fas fa-motorcycle"></i> </div> <div style="position:absolute;top:-12px;left:50%;transform:translateX(-50%) rotate(${bearing}deg);transform-origin:50% 30px;z-index:201"> <div style="width:0;height:0;border-left:10px solid transparent;border-right:10px solid transparent;border-bottom:16px solid #FF6B00;filter:drop-shadow(0 2px 4px rgba(0,0,0,.4))"></div> </div> </div> <div style="position:absolute;left:50%;top:100%;transform:translate(-50%,4px);background:linear-gradient(135deg,#FF6B00,#FF1744);color:#fff;padding:3px 8px;border-radius:99px;font-size:9px;font-weight:800;white-space:nowrap">${CURRENT_LANG==='ar'?'أنا':'Sie'}</div> </div> <div style="position:absolute;left:calc(50% + ${driverLeft}px);top:calc(50% + ${driverTop}px);width:60px;height:60px;border-radius:50%;background:rgba(255,107,0,.3);z-index:198;transform:translate(-50%,-50%);animation:bgDriverRipple 2s ease-out infinite"></div>`; } // Quick rule snippets (embedded for easy copy-paste) const FBR_FIRESTORE_RULES = `rules_version = '2'; service cloud.firestore { match /databases/{database}/documents { function isSignedIn() { return request.auth != null; } function hasRole(role) { return isSignedIn() && exists(/databases/$(database)/documents/users/$(request.auth.uid)) && get(/databases/$(database)/documents/users/$(request.auth.uid)).data.role == role; } function isCustomer() { return hasRole('customer'); } function isDriver() { return hasRole('driver'); } function isAdmin() { return hasRole('admin'); } function isOwner(uid) { return isSignedIn() && request.auth.uid == uid; } function orderValid(data) { return data.keys().hasAll(['id','customerId','status','total','items','createdAt']) && data.status in ['pending','preparing','delivering','delivered','cancelled'] && data.total is number && data.total >= 0 && data.total <= 10000 && data.items is list && data.items.size() <= 100; } match /users/{uid} { allow read: if isSignedIn(); allow create: if isOwner(uid); allow update: if isOwner(uid) || isAdmin(); allow delete: if isAdmin(); } match /orders/{orderId} { allow read: if isSignedIn() && ( isAdmin() || (isCustomer() && resource.data.customerId == request.auth.uid) || (isDriver() && (resource.data.status in ['pending','preparing','delivering','delivered'] || resource.data.driverId == request.auth.uid)) ); allow create: if isSignedIn() && request.resource.data.customerId == request.auth.uid && request.resource.data.status == 'pending' && orderValid(request.resource.data); allow update: if isSignedIn() && ( isAdmin() || (isCustomer() && resource.data.customerId == request.auth.uid && request.resource.data.status == 'cancelled' && resource.data.status == 'pending') || (isDriver() && (resource.data.driverId == request.auth.uid || resource.data.status == 'pending') && request.resource.data.status in ['pending','preparing','delivering','delivered','cancelled'] && orderValid(request.resource.data)) ); allow delete: if isAdmin(); } match /notifications/{notifId} { allow read: if isSignedIn() && resource.data.userId == request.auth.uid; allow create: if isSignedIn() && request.resource.data.userId == request.auth.uid; allow update: if isSignedIn() && resource.data.userId == request.auth.uid; allow delete: if isSignedIn() && resource.data.userId == request.auth.uid; } match /drivers/{driverId} { allow read: if isSignedIn(); allow write: if isSignedIn() && (request.auth.uid == driverId || isAdmin()); } match /coupons/{couponId} { allow read: if isSignedIn(); allow write: if isAdmin(); } match /products/{productId} { allow read: if true; allow write: if isAdmin(); } match /{document=**} { allow read, write: if false; } } }`; const FBR_STORAGE_RULES = `rules_version = '2'; service firebase.storage { match /b/{bucket}/o { match /avatars/{userId}.jpg { allow read: if true; allow write: if request.auth != null && request.auth.uid == userId && request.resource.size < 5 * 1024 * 1024 && request.resource.contentType.matches('image/.*'); } match /delivery_photos/{orderId}.jpg { allow read: if request.auth != null; allow write: if request.auth != null && request.resource.size < 8 * 1024 * 1024 && request.resource.contentType.matches('image/.*'); } match /products/{productId}.jpg { allow read: if true; allow write: if request.auth != null && request.resource.size < 8 * 1024 * 1024 && request.resource.contentType.matches('image/.*'); } match /{path=**} { allow read, write: if false; } } }`; window.__copyRulesToClipboard = function(type){ const isFB = type === 'firestore'; const txt = isFB ? FBR_FIRESTORE_RULES : FBR_STORAGE_RULES; const L = CURRENT_LANG === 'ar'; // Try Clipboard API if(navigator.clipboard && navigator.clipboard.writeText){ navigator.clipboard.writeText(txt).then(() => { showToast(L?'✅ تم النسخ! الصقه في Firebase Console':'✅ Kopiert! In Firebase Console einfügen'); }).catch(() => fallbackCopy(txt, L)); } else { fallbackCopy(txt, L); } }; function fallbackCopy(text, L){ const ta = document.createElement('textarea'); ta.value = text; ta.style.position = 'fixed'; ta.style.left = '-9999px'; document.body.appendChild(ta); ta.select(); try{ document.execCommand('copy'); showToast(L?'✅ تم النسخ':'✅ Kopiert'); } catch(e){ showToast(L?'❌ فشل النسخ':'❌ Kopieren fehlgeschlagen'); } document.body.removeChild(ta); } // Run a live security check against Firestore async function runSecurityCheck(){ const L = CURRENT_LANG === 'ar'; const el = document.getElementById('bgSecurityCheckResult'); if(!el) return; el.style.display = 'block'; el.style.background = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)'; el.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin"></i> ' + (L?'جاري الفحص الأمني...':'Sicherheitscheck läuft...'); const results = []; // 1. } function filterAdminOrders(status){ const tbody = $('adminOrdersTbody'); if(!tbody) return; const filtered = status==='all' ? state.orders : state.orders.filter(o=>o.status===status); if(!filtered.length){ tbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="8" style="text-align:center;padding:30px;color:var(--text-muted)">${CURRENT_LANG==='ar'?'لا توجد طلبات':'Keine Bestellungen'}</td></tr>`; } /* ============================================================ AUDIO (WebAudio synth — no external file needed) ============================================================ */ let _audioCtx = null; function audio(){ if(!_audioCtx){ try{ _audioCtx = new (window.AudioContext||window.webkitAudioContext)(); }catch(e){ return null; } } if(_audioCtx.state==='suspended') _audioCtx.resume(); return _audioCtx; } function beep(freq=440, dur=300, vol=0.3, type='sine'){ const ctx = audio(); if(!ctx) return; const o = ctx.createOscillator(); const g = ctx.createGain(); o.type = type; o.frequency.value = freq; o.connect(g); g.connect(ctx.destination); g.gain.setValueAtTime(0, ctx.currentTime); g.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(vol, ctx.currentTime+0.02); g.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0, ctx.currentTime+dur/1000); o.start(); o.stop(ctx.currentTime+dur/1000); } /* Loud attention sound — used for driver new order */ function playIncomingBeep(){ // three tones ascending beep(660, 200, 0.4, 'square'); setTimeout(()=>beep(880, 200, 0.4, 'square'), 220); setTimeout(()=>beep(1100, 300, 0.4, 'square'), 440); // vibration (mobile) if(navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate([200,100,200,100,400]); } /* ============================================================ BUSINESS LOGIC ============================================================ */ function addToCart(id){ // Find product to grab its price + name id = String(id || ''); async function bgAdminAddAddress(geocodeToo){ const isAr = CURRENT_LANG === 'ar'; const label = document.getElementById('bgNewAddrLabel')?.value?.trim(); const type = document.getElementById('bgNewAddrType')?.value; const country = document.getElementById('bgNewAddrCountry')?.value?.trim()?.toUpperCase() || 'DE'; const city = document.getElementById('bgNewAddrCity')?.value?.trim(); const address = document.getElementById('bgNewAddrFull')?.value?.trim(); if(!label || !address){ showToast(isAr?'املأ الاسم والعنوان':'Name und Adresse erforderlich'); return; } let lat = null, lng = null; if(geocodeToo){ showToast(isAr?'⏳ جاري جلب الإحداثيات...':'⏳ Koordinaten werden abgerufen...'); const result = await bgGeocodeAddress(address); if(result){ lat = result.lat; lng = result.lng; } else { showToast(isAr?'❌ ما قدرنا نلقى العنوان - حدد الإحداثيات يدوياً':'❌ Adresse nicht gefunden – Koordinaten manuell eingeben'); } } if(lat === null || lng === null){ // Ask for lat/lng manually (v4.97 hardening — themed modal) const llInput = await bgCustomPrompt( isAr ? 'الإحداثيات (lat,lng) مثال: 50.9375,6.9603' : 'Koordinaten (lat,lng) z.B. 50.9375,6.9603', '50.9375,6.9603', { title: isAr ? 'إحداثيات العنوان' : 'Adress-Koordinaten' } ); if(llInput == null || !String(llInput).trim()) return; const parts = String(llInput).split(',').map(s => parseFloat(s.trim())); if(parts.length !== 2 || isNaN(parts[0]) || isNaN(parts[1])){ showToast(isAr?'❌ إحداثيات غير صحيحة':'❌ Ungültige Koordinaten'); return; } lat = parts[0]; lng = parts[1]; } const list = bgGetAddresses(); const newAddr = { id: 'custom-' + Date.now() + '-' + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2,6), label, country, city, address, lat, lng, type }; list.push(newAddr); bgSaveAddresses(list); showToast(isAr?'✅ تم إضافة العنوان':'✅ Adresse hinzugefügt'); if(window.BLINKGO_AUDIO?.success) window.BLINKGO_AUDIO.success(); setActivePage('admin-addresses'); } async function bgAdminDeleteAddress(id){ const ok = await bgCustomConfirm( CURRENT_LANG==='ar' ? 'حذف هذا العنوان؟' : 'Diese Adresse löschen?', { title: CURRENT_LANG==='ar' ? '🗑️ حذف' : '🗑️ Löschen' } ); if(!ok) return; const list = bgGetAddresses().filter(a => a.id !== id); bgSaveAddresses(list); showToast(CURRENT_LANG==='ar'?'🗑️ تم الحذف':'🗑️ Gelöscht'); setActivePage('admin-addresses'); } window.bgAdminAddAddress = bgAdminAddAddress; window.bgAdminDeleteAddress = bgAdminDeleteAddress; // === TRACK PAGE: Address search → show on live map === async function bgTrackSearchAddress(){ const isAr = CURRENT_LANG === 'ar'; const input = document.getElementById('bgTrackAddrInput'); const q = input?.value?.trim(); if(!q){ showToast(isAr?'اكتب عنوان للبحث':'Bitte Adresse eingeben'); return; } showToast(isAr?'⏳ جاري البحث...':'⏳ Suche läuft...'); const result = await bgGeocodeAddress(q); if(!result){ showToast(isAr?'❌ ما لقينا العنوان':'❌ Adresse nicht gefunden'); return; } // Show result banner const resultDiv = document.getElementById('bgTrackAddrResult'); if(resultDiv){ resultDiv.style.display = 'block'; resultDiv.innerHTML = ` <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px;flex-wrap:wrap"> <i class="fas fa-map-marker-alt" style="color:var(--primary);font-size:18px"></i> <div style="flex:1;min-width:0"> <div style="font-weight:700">${result.formatted_address || q}</div> <div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-muted)">${result.lat.toFixed(5)}, ${result.lng.toFixed(5)} · ${result.source === 'google' ? 'Google' : 'OSM'}</div> </div> <button class="btn btn-sm btn-secondary" onclick="bgTrackClearAddress()" style="padding:4px 8px"> <i class="fas fa-times"></i> </button> </div> `; } // Save the searched location try { localStorage.setItem('bg_user_location', JSON.stringify({lat: result.lat, lng: result.lng, label: result.formatted_address || q, formatted_address: result.formatted_address})); } catch(_){} // Update the Leaflet map: re-init to show this location with the customer marker const mapDiv = document.getElementById('bgCustomerMap'); if(mapDiv){ // If we have a Leaflet map, just re-center it if(window.__bgMap && typeof L !== 'undefined'){ try { window.__bgMap.setView([result.lat, result.lng], 15);
