============================================================ LIVE TRACKING HELPERS ============================================================ */ function _seedDriverLocations(){ if(Object.keys(state.driverLocations).length) return; DRIVERS.forEach((d,i)=>{ state.driverLocations[d.id] = { x: 20 + (i*15)%60, y: 30 + (i*23)%50, targetX: 20 + (i*15)%60, targetY: 30 + (i*23)%50 }; }); } function _tickDriverLocations(){ // move online drivers slowly toward new random positions _seedDriverLocations(); DRIVERS.forEach(d=>{ if(!d.online) return; const loc = state.driverLocations[d.id]; if(!loc) return; loc.targetX = Math.max(10, Math.min(90, loc.targetX + (Math.random()-0.5)*30)); loc.targetY = Math.max(15, Math.min(85, loc.targetY + (Math.random()-0.5)*30)); loc.x += (loc.targetX - loc.x) * 0.3; loc.y += (loc.targetY - loc.y) * 0.3; }); } function _startLocationTicker(){ if(window._locTickerStarted) return; _seedDriverLocations(); window._locTickerStarted = true; setInterval(()=>{ _tickDriverLocations(); // re-render only when on relevant pages if(state.page==='admin-dashboard' || state.page==='track'){ renderPageContent(); } }, 2500); } /* ============================================================ LIVE CHAT SYSTEM ============================================================ */ function _chatKey(otherName){ const me = state.user ? (state.user.id||state.user.name) : 'anon'; return 'chat_' + [me, otherName].sort().join('_'); } function _getThread(key){ if(!state.chatMessages[key]){ state.chatMessages[key] = [ { from:'system', text:CURRENT_LANG==='ar'?'بدأت المحادثة':'Chat gestartet', time:Date.now() } ]; } return state.chatMessages[key]; } function _renderChatMsg(m){ const t = new Date(m.time).toLocaleTimeString('ar-SA',{hour:'2-digit',minute:'2-digit'}); if(m.from==='system') return `<div class="chat-msg system">${m.text}</div>`; return `<div class="chat-msg ${m.from==='me'?'me':'them'}">${m.text}<span class="chat-time">${t}</span></div>`; } function openChat(otherName, otherRole){ const key = _chatKey(otherName); const thread = _getThread(key); const old = document.getElementById('chatModal'); if(old) old.remove(); const initials = (otherName||'?').split(' ').map(x=>x[0]).join('').substring(0,2); const roleLabel = otherRole==='driver'?(CURRENT_LANG==='ar'?'سائق':'Fahrer'):otherRole==='admin'?(CURRENT_LANG==='ar'?'دعم':'Admin'):(CURRENT_LANG==='ar'?'عميل':'Kunde'); const m = document.createElement('div'); m.id = 'chatModal'; m.className = 'chat-backdrop'; m.innerHTML = ` <div class="chat-box" onclick="event.stopPropagation()"> <div class="chat-header"> <div class="avatar">${initials}</div> <div class="info"> <div class="name">${otherName}</div> <div class="status">${roleLabel} • ${CURRENT_LANG==='ar'?'متصل':'Online'}</div> </div> <button class="chat-close" onclick="document.getElementById('chatModal').remove()"><i class="fas fa-times"></i></button> </div> <div class="chat-body" id="chatBody">${thread.map(_renderChatMsg).join('')}</div> <div class="chat-input"> <input type="text" id="chatInput" placeholder="اكتب رسder تك..." onkeydown="if(event.key==='Enter')sendChatMsg('${key.replace(/'/g,"\\'")}','${otherName.replace(/'/g,"\\'")}')"> <button onclick="sendChatMsg('${key.replace(/'/g,"\\'")}','${otherName.replace(/'/g,"\\'")}')"><i class="fas fa-paper-plane"></i></button> </div> </div>`; document.body.appendChild(m); setTimeout(()=>{ const b=$('chatBody'); if(b) b.scrollTop=b.scrollHeight; }, 50); // auto-reply simulation m.addEventListener('click', e=>{ if(e.target===m) m.remove(); }); } function sendChatMsg(key, otherName){ const input = $('chatInput'); const txt = (input?.value||'').trim(); if(!txt) return; _checkBadges(); const thread = _getThread(key); thread.push({ from:'me', text:txt, time:Date.now() }); if(input) input.value = ''; const body = $('chatBody'); if(body){ body.innerHTML = thread.map(_renderChatMsg).join(''); body.scrollTop = body.scrollHeight; } // simulate reply const replies = CURRENT_LANG==='ar' ?['تمام 👍','حاضر','وصلت','في الطريق','قريباً','تمام تم','موافق ✅','عندي سؤال ثاني','هل تحتاج شي ثاني؟','بخدمتك'] :['Alles klar 👍','Verstanden','Bin da','Unterwegs','In Kürze','Erledigt','Passt ✅','Noch eine Frage','Brauchst du noch was?','Gerne']; setTimeout(()=>{ thread.push({ from:'them', text:replies[Math.floor(Math.random()*replies.length)], time:Date.now() }); const b2 = $('chatBody'); if(b2){ b2.innerHTML = thread.map(_renderChatMsg).join(''); b2.scrollTop = b2.scrollHeight; } }, 900 + Math.random()*900); } /* ============================================================ ADMIN SIMULATION ============================================================ */ function enterSimulation(targetRole){ if(!state.user || state.user.role!=='admin'){ showToast(CURRENT_LANG==='ar'?'❌ هذه الميزة للمدير فقط':'❌ Nur für Administrator'); } function _yesterdayKey(){ const d = new Date(); d.setDate(d.getDate()-1); return d.toISOString().slice(0,10); } function _calcCheckinReward(streak){ // returns points for the day based on streak length if(streak % 30 === 0 && streak > 0) return 200; } /* ============================================================ WALLET / CASHBACK ============================================================ */ const _CASHBACK_RATE = 0.05; // 5% cashback function _loadWallet(){ try{ const w = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('bg_wallet')||'null'); _saveWallet(); return cb; } function debitWallet(amount, orderId){ if(state.wallet.balance < amount){ return false; } state.wallet.balance -= amount; state.wallet.tx.unshift({ id:Date.now()+Math.random(), type:'debit', amount, orderId, time:Date.now() }); state.wallet.tx = state.wallet.tx.slice(0, 50); _saveWallet(); return true; } function _walletTxIcon(t){ return t.type==='cashback'?'fa-plus-circle':'fa-minus-circle'; } function _walletTxLabel(t){ if(t.type==='cashback') return `Cashback ${t.orderId?'#'+String(t.orderId).slice(-6):''}`; 'de' : 'ar'); try{ window.scrollTo({top:0,behavior:'smooth'}); }catch(e){} } /* ============================================================ FIREBASE HELPERS (Auth + Firestore) ============================================================ */ // Detect if Firebase is configured and reachable let FIREBASE_READY = false; async function _fbCheckReady(){ if(!firebaseDB || !firebaseAuth){ FIREBASE_READY = false; return false; } try{ // Hard 1.2s timeout — if Firebase is slow, fall back to local const timeout = new Promise((_, rej) => setTimeout(() => rej(new Error('firebase-timeout')), 1200)); return true; }catch(e){ FIREBASE_READY = false; console.warn('[Firebase] ⚠️ Database not reachable, using local mode only:', e.code || e.message); return false; } } // Demo accounts shared across devices for cross-device testing const DEMO_ACCOUNTS = { customer: { email:'demo-customer@blink-go.app', password:'demo123', name:'عميل تجريبي', phone:'0500000001', role:'customer' }, driver: { email:'demo-driver@blink-go.app', password:'demo123', name:'سائق تجريبي', phone:'0500000002', role:'driver' }, admin: { email:'demo-admin@blink-go.app', password:'demo123', name:'Administrator تجريبي', phone:'0500000003', role:'admin' } }; async function _fbSignIn(email, password){ if(!firebaseAuth) throw new Error('Firebase غير مهيأ'); const cred = await firebaseAuth.signInWithEmailAndPassword(email, password); return cred.user; } async function _fbRegister(email, password, userData){ if(!firebaseAuth) throw new Error('Firebase غير مهيأ'); const cred = await firebaseAuth.createUserWithEmailAndPassword(email, password); await firebaseDB.collection('users').doc(cred.user.uid).set({ ...userData, email, uid: cred.user.uid, createdAt: firebase.firestore.FieldValue.serverTimestamp() }); return cred.user; } async function _fbSignOut(){ if(firebaseAuth) await firebaseAuth.signOut(); } async function _fbGetUser(uid){ if(!firebaseDB) return null; try{ const snap = await firebaseDB.collection('users').doc(uid).get(); return snap.exists ? { id: snap.id, ...snap.data() } : null; }catch(e){ console.warn('_fbGetUser failed:', e.code || e.message); return null; } } async function _fbEnsureDemoAccount(role){ const acc = DEMO_ACCOUNTS[role]; } } // ===== Firestore: Orders ===== async function _fbCreateOrder(order){ if(!firebaseDB) throw new Error('Firebase غير مهيأ'); const ref = await firebaseDB.collection('orders').add({ ...order, createdAt: firebase.firestore.FieldValue.serverTimestamp() }); return ref.id; } // === SHARE ORDER VIA URL FALLBACK === // If Firebase doesn't work (rules block, network down), the customer gets a shareable link // containing the order data. The driver opens the link to import the order. function generateShareOrderUrl(order){ try { // Encode the order data as base64 const json = JSON.stringify({ id: order.id, customerId: order.customerId, customerName: order.customerName, customerPhone: order.customerPhone, items: order.items, total: order.total, address: order.address, merchant: order.merchant, pay: order.pay, tip: order.tip, date: order.date, createdAt: order.createdAt }); const encoded = btoa(unescape(encodeURIComponent(json))); const baseUrl = window.location.origin + window.location.pathname; return baseUrl + '#import=' + encoded; } catch(e){ console.error('generateShareOrderUrl:', e); return null; } } window.generateShareOrderUrl = generateShareOrderUrl; // === CARD PAYMENT HELPERS === // Format card number with spaces every 4 digits function bgFormatCardNumber(input){ let v = input.value.replace(/\D/g,''); v = v.substring(0, 19); const parts = v.match(/.{1,4}/g); input.value = parts ? parts.join(' ') : ''; // Detect brand const brand = bgDetectCardBrand(v); const icon = document.getElementById('bgCardBrandIcon'); if(icon){ if(brand === 'visa'){ icon.className = 'fab fa-cc-visa'; icon.style.color = '#1A1F71'; } else if(brand === 'mastercard'){ icon.className = 'fab fa-cc-mastercard'; icon.style.color = '#EB001B'; } else if(brand === 'amex'){ icon.className = 'fab fa-cc-amex'; icon.style.color = '#006FCF'; } else { icon.className = 'fas fa-credit-card'; icon.style.color = 'var(--text-muted)'; } } } window.bgFormatCardNumber = bgFormatCardNumber; function bgDetectCardBrand(num){ if(/^4/.test(num)) return 'visa'; if(/^(5[1-5]|2[2-7])/.test(num)) return 'mastercard'; if(/^3[47]/.test(num)) return 'amex'; return 'unknown'; } window.bgDetectCardBrand = bgDetectCardBrand; // Luhn algorithm for card validation function bgLuhnCheck(num){ let sum = 0; let shouldDouble = false; for(let i = num.length - 1; i >= 0; i--){ let digit = parseInt(num.charAt(i), 10); if(shouldDouble){ digit *= 2; if(digit > 9) digit -= 9; } sum += digit; shouldDouble = !shouldDouble; } return sum % 10 === 0; } window.bgLuhnCheck = bgLuhnCheck; function bgValidateCard(input){ const num = input.value.replace(/\s/g, ''); if(num && !bgLuhnCheck(num)){ input.style.borderColor = '#F44336'; return false; } else { input.style.borderColor = num ? '#4CAF50' : 'var(--border)'; return true; } } window.bgValidateCard = bgValidateCard; function bgFormatExpiry(input){ let v = input.value.replace(/\D/g,''); if(v.length >= 2){ v = v.substring(0,2) + '/' + v.substring(2,4); } input.value = v; } window.bgFormatExpiry = bgFormatExpiry; function bgProcessCardPayment(){ // For Stripe Checkout, we redirect to hosted page — no card input needed here // Just trigger the real payment flow return true; } window.bgProcessCardPayment = bgProcessCardPayment; // === STRIPE CHECKOUT REDIRECT === // Creates a Stripe Checkout Session via Cloudflare Worker and redirects async function bgRedirectToStripeCheckout(amount, orderId, description){ try { // Default Worker URL (configured for blinkgo.de domain) const DEFAULT_WORKER_URL = 'https://stripe.blinkgo.de'; const workerUrl = localStorage.getItem('bg_stripe_worker_url') || DEFAULT_WORKER_URL; if(!workerUrl){ showToast(CURRENT_LANG==='ar'? '❌ عيّن رابط Stripe Worker في الإعدادات أولاً': '❌ Bitte zuerst Stripe-Worker-URL in den Einstellungen setzen'); // Themed modal (v4.97 hardening — no native prompt()) const url = await bgCustomPrompt( CURRENT_LANG==='ar' ? 'أدخل رابط Stripe Worker (من Cloudflare):' : 'Stripe Worker URL eingeben (von Cloudflare):', 'https://stripe.blinkgo.de', { title: CURRENT_LANG==='ar' ? '⚙️ إعداد Stripe Worker' : '⚙️ Stripe Worker Setup', okLabel: CURRENT_LANG==='ar' ? 'حفظ' : 'Speichern' } ); if(url && String(url).startsWith('https://')){ localStorage.setItem('bg_stripe_worker_url', String(url)); showToast(CURRENT_LANG==='ar'?'✅ تم الحفظ':'✅ Gespeichert'); // Try again return bgRedirectToStripeCheckout(amount, orderId, description); } return false; } showToast(CURRENT_LANG==='ar'?'🔄 جاري التحويل لـ Stripe...':'🔄 Weiterleitung zu Stripe...'); // amount is already in EUROS from bgDoCheckout. Worker will multiply by 100 to get cents. const totalEuros = Number(amount); // Stripe minimum is €0.50 — enforce floor if(!isFinite(totalEuros) || totalEuros < 0.50){ showToast(CURRENT_LANG==='ar'? `❌ الحد الأدنى للطلب €0.50 (حالياً €${totalEuros.toFixed(2)})`: `❌ Mindestbestellwert €0.50 (aktuell €${totalEuros.toFixed(2)})`); return false; } // Call the worker const response = await fetch(workerUrl + '/create-checkout', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ amount: totalEuros, orderId: orderId, customerName: state.user?.name || '', customerEmail: state.user?.email || '', description: description || `BlinkGo Bestellung #${orderId.slice(-6)}`, successUrl: window.location.origin + window.location.pathname, cancelUrl: window.location.origin + window.location.pathname }) }); if(!response.ok){ const err = await response.json().catch(() => ({})); showToast(CURRENT_LANG==='ar'?`❌ ${err.error||'خطأ Stripe'}`:`❌ ${err.error||'Stripe-Fehler'}`); return false; } const data = await response.json(); if(!data.url){ showToast(CURRENT_LANG==='ar'?'❌ لم يتم إنشاء جلسة الدفع':'❌ Keine Checkout-URL'); return false; } // Save order ID to confirm payment on return sessionStorage.setItem('bg_pending_payment_order', orderId); sessionStorage.setItem('bg_pending_payment_url', data.url); // Redirect to Stripe window.location.href = data.url; return true; } catch(e){ console.error('bgRedirectToStripeCheckout:', e); showToast(CURRENT_LANG==='ar'?`❌ خطأ: ${e.message}`:`❌ Fehler: ${e.message}`); return false; } } window.bgRedirectToStripeCheckout = bgRedirectToStripeCheckout; // === CHECK FOR STRIPE RETURN === // When user comes back from Stripe Checkout, verify payment and update order async function checkStripeReturn(){ const url = new URL(window.location.href); const success = url.searchParams.get('stripe_success'); const cancel = url.searchParams.get('stripe_cancel'); const orderId = url.searchParams.get('orderId'); const sessionId = url.searchParams.get('session_id'); if(!success && !cancel) return; if(success && orderId){ // Verify the payment with the worker const workerUrl = localStorage.getItem('bg_stripe_worker_url') || ''; let paid = true; if(workerUrl && sessionId){ try { const r = await fetch(workerUrl + '/verify?session_id=' + encodeURIComponent(sessionId)); const data = await r.json(); paid = data.paymentStatus === 'paid'; } catch(e){ console.warn('Verify payment:', e); } } if(paid){ // Mark order as paid const o = state.orders.find(x => String(x.id) === String(orderId)); } } catch(_){} } } } else if(cancel && orderId){ showToast(CURRENT_LANG==='ar'?'⚠️ تم إلغاء الدفع':'⚠️ Zahlung abgebrochen'); // Clean URL history.replaceState(null, '', window.location.pathname); } // Remove pending payment sessionStorage.removeItem('bg_pending_payment_order'); async function _fbUpdateOrder(orderId, updates){ if(!firebaseDB) return; await firebaseDB.collection('orders').doc(String(orderId)).update(updates); } function _fbSubscribeOrders(callback, role, userId){ if(!firebaseDB) return ()=>{};
